
# Fonts supported by *that terminal*

Most of these fonts are Public Domain, and come from X11. Exceptions are
listed.


## Font 4x5

X11 font “micro”.

#### Basic Latin

    U+0020..U+003F  !"#$%&'()*+,-./0123456789:;<=>?
    U+0040..U+005F @ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ[\]^_
    U+0060..U+007E `abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz{|}~ 

#### Latin-1 Supplement


Supported only by approximation:

    U+00A0..U+00BF  ¡¢£ ¥¦  ©ª«¬­®  ±²³´µ ·¸¹º»¼½¾ 
    U+00C0..U+00DF ÀÁÂÃÄÅÆÇÈÉÊËÌÍÎÏÐÑÒÓÔÕÖ×ØÙÚÛÜÝÞß
    U+00E0..U+00FF àáâãäåæçèéêëìíîïðñòóôõö÷øùúûüýþÿ

X11 misc-fixed font. Pairs perfectly with 12x13.

    U+1EE00..U+1EE1F 𞸀𞸁𞸂𞸃 𞸅𞸆𞸇𞸈𞸉𞸊𞸋𞸌𞸍𞸎𞸏𞸐𞸑𞸒𞸓𞸔𞸕𞸖𞸗𞸘𞸙𞸚𞸛

## Font 9x18

X11 misc-fixed font. Pairs perfectly with 18x18.
